<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пологий.html>поло́гий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pológij</span>) (<i>rare/awkward comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)поло́же</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>gentle, gently sloping
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пологий.html>поло́гий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:берег.html>бе́рег</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pológij</b> béreg</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sloping bank/shore</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***положение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:положение.html>положе́ние</a> (546)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:положить.html>положи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">položítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to put, to lay</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:положение.html>положе́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">položénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:положение.html>положе́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:положение.html>положе́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:положение.html>положе́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>position, location</li>
<li>situation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">па́товое <b><a href = vnd.unilang:положение.html>положе́ние</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pátovoje <b>položénije</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chess</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> stalemate</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">stalemate situation</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>state, condition
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:интересный.html>интере́сном</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:положение.html>положе́нии</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">euphemism</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v interésnom položénii</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pregnant</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">in an interesting state</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>standing</li>
<li>thesis</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><span class="deprecated-label">plural</span></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> regulations</li></ol>

***положить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:положить.html>положи́ть</a> (519)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ложи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ložítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:положить.html>положи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">položítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:класть.html>класть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to put, to lay, to lay down, to deposit
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:положить.html>положи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:конец.html>коне́ц</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:страдание.html>страда́ниям</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>položítʹ</b> konéc stradánijam</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to put end to the sufferings</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to apply</li>
<li>to spend</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The imperfective form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ложи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ložítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<i>without any prefixes and reflexive suffixes</i>) is considered non-standard in the modern Russian, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:класть.html>класть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klastʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> should be used instead.</li></ul>

***полоз.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:полоз.html>по́лоз</a> (18169)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*polzъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полоз.html>по́лоз</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">póloz</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полоз.html>по́лоза</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полоз.html>поло́зья</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полоз.html>поло́зьев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sled runner
<ul><li><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white"><a href = vnd.unilang:лев.html>Лев</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:толстый.html>То́лстой</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяин.html>Хозя́ин</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работник.html>рабо́тник</a></i> 1895:<dl><dd><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добрый.html>до́брый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жеребец.html>жеребе́ц</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:легкое.html>лёгким</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:скрип.html>скри́пом</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:полоз.html>поло́зьев</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сдвинуть.html>сдви́нул</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сани.html>са́ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бойкий.html>бо́йкой</a> хо́дою <a href = vnd.unilang:тронуться.html>тро́нулся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:накатанный.html>нака́танной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поселок.html>посёлке</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:морозный.html>моро́зной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́ге</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Dóbryj žerebéc s ljóxkim skrípom <b>polózʹjev</b> sdvínul sáni i bójkoj xódoju trónulsja po nakátannoj v posjólke moróznoj doróge</i></dd><dd>The obedient horse pushed the sled, whose <b>runners</b> coyly queaked, and with pert trot began marching the frozen hamlet road</dd></dl></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">technical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a smooth, flat surface, bent upwards in the front and meant for sliding, such as a sled runner</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поломать.html>полома́ть</a> (9214)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ломать.html>лома́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lomátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поломать.html>полома́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">polomátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ломать.html>лома́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to break, to fracture</li>
<li>to rack, to cause to ache</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:полоскать.html>поло́сканный</a> (16778)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полоскать.html>поло́сканный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">polóskannyj</span>)

</p>

***полотенце.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:полотенце.html>полоте́нце</a> (3399)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полотно.html>полотно́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">polotnó</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">canvas</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-це</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ce</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">платьньце</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">platĭnĭce</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">पट</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">paṭa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cloth, garment</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полотенце.html>полоте́нце</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poloténce</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полотенце.html>полоте́нца</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полотенце.html>полоте́нца</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полотенце.html>полоте́нец</a></b>)
</p>

***полотно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:полотно.html>полотно́</a> (4959)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*poltьno</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*polto-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cloth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:платный.html>платно́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">platnó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from Old Church Slavonic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полотно.html>полотно́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">polotnó</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полотно.html>полотна́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полотно.html>поло́тна</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полотно.html>поло́тен</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>linen</li>
<li>cloth, bunting</li>
<li>canvas</li>
<li>roadbed <i>(of a railroad)</i>; embankment</li>
<li>saw web, saw blade</li>
<li>panel</li>
<li>picture, painting</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полотнище.html>поло́тнище</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">polótnišče</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pèlti</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:полтинник.html>полти́нник</a> (15491)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полтинник.html>полти́нник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poltínnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полтинник.html>полти́нника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полтинник.html>полти́нники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полтинник.html>полти́нников</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fifty copecks</li>
<li>fifty-copeck piece</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> age of fifty</li></ol>

***полтора.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:полтора.html>полтора́</a> (1401)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пол-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pol-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">half</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:второй.html>второ́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vtorój</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">second</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*роlъ vъtora</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">half of the second</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">półtora</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полтора.html>полтора́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poltorá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полтора.html>полторы́</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poltorý</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>one and a half (1½), sesqui-
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:полтора.html>полтора́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рубля́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poltorá</b> rubljá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">1.5 roubles</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полтора.html>полторы́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:минута.html>мину́ты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">poltorý minúty</i> ― <span class="e-translation">1.5 minutes</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:полтора.html>полу́тора</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рубле́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">iz <b>polútora</b> rubléj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">from 1.5 roubles</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:полтора.html>полу́тора</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рубля́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">k <b>polútora</b> rubljám</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to 1.5 roubles</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:полтора.html>полу́тора</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рубля́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>polútora</b> rubljámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with 1.5 roubles</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:полтора.html>полу́тора</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рубля́х</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">o <b>polútora</b> rubljáx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">concerning 1.5 roubles</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In the nominative and accusative, this number governs the genitive <b>singular</b> of the noun. In all of the other cases, it governs the <b>plural</b> of the noun.
</p>
